It is a number associated with a particular type of food to indicate the food's effect on a person's blood glucose (blood sugar) level. \r\n\r\nThe Glycemic Load (GL) of food is a number that estimates how much the food will raise a person's blood glucose level after eating it. \r\n\r\nBecause GL is related to the food's effect on blood sugar, low-GL meals are often recommended for diabetic control and weight loss.\r\n\r\nDid you know that recent studies from the Harvard School of Public Health indicate that the risks of diseases such as type 2 diabetes and coronary heart disease are strongly related to the GI of the overall diet. The Shanghai Women's Health Study concluded that women whose diets had the highest glycemic index were 21 percent more likely to develop type 2 diabetes than women whose diets had the lowest glycemic index.
